# <a name="payment-thresholds-methods-and-timeframes"></a><span data-ttu-id="769dc-103">支払しきい値、方法、期間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-103">Payment thresholds, methods, and timeframes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="769dc-104">支払の送金にかかる推定時間、支払しきい値、および支払を受けることができる Microsoft マーケットプレースは、お住まいの国/地域および受取りアカウントの種類によって異なる可能性があります。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-104">The estimated time to transfer payments, applicable payment threshold(s), and Microsoft marketplaces from which you can receive payments can vary depending on your country/region and payout account type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="769dc-105">このトピックでは、国/地域ごとにサポートされている支払しきい値と支払方法について説明します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-105">This topic outlines the payment thresholds and payment methods supported in each country/region.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="769dc-106">どのような国/地域であっても、ACH/SEPA または電信送金を使用して支払を行います。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-106">For any given country/region, we will either use ACH/SEPA or wire transfer to deliver our payments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="769dc-107">さらに、一部の国/地域では、支払方法として PayPal をサポートします。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-107">Additionally, some countries/regions support PayPal as a payment method.</span></span>

## <a name="number-of-days-for-payments-to-reach-payout-account"></a><span data-ttu-id="769dc-108">支払が受取りアカウントに到着するまでの日数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-108">Number of days for payments to reach payout account</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="769dc-109">通常、支払は、該当する月の 15 日に行われますが、支払が受取りアカウントに到着するまでさらに時間がかかります。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-109">We'll typically send any payment due in a given month by the 15th day of that month, but it will take additional time for the payment to reach your account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="769dc-110">日数は、以下に示すように、アカウントで使用する支払方法によって異なります。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-110">The amount of days will vary depending on the payment method we use for your account, as described below.</span></span> 

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="769dc-111">以下に示す日数は概算値です。いずれの支払も、より長い日数または短い日数になる可能性があります。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-111">The days shown below are approximate; any given payout may take a longer or shorter amount of time.</span></span>


| <span data-ttu-id="769dc-112">支払方法</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-112">Payment method</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="769dc-113">受取りアカウントに到着するまでの日数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-113">Number of days to reach payout account</span></span>     |
|--------------------|--------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="769dc-114">PayPal</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-114">PayPal</span></span>             | <span data-ttu-id="769dc-115">1 営業日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-115">1 business day</span></span>                             | 
| <span data-ttu-id="769dc-116">ACH/SEPA</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-116">ACH/SEPA</span></span>           | <span data-ttu-id="769dc-117">2 ～ 3 営業日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-117">2-3 business days</span></span>                          |
| <span data-ttu-id="769dc-118">電信送金</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-118">Wire Transfer</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="769dc-119">7 ～ 10 営業日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-119">7-10 business days</span></span>                         |

&nbsp;

<span data-ttu-id="769dc-120">これらの支払方法が各マーケットプレースで使用されている国/地域を確認するには、以下の表をご覧ください。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-120">To see the countries/regions in which these payment methods are used for each marketplace, review the tables below.</span></span>

## <a name="payment-thresholds-and-methods"></a><span data-ttu-id="769dc-121">支払のしきい値と方法</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-121">Payment thresholds and methods</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="769dc-122">この支払しきい値は米ドル (USD) で記載されています。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-122">Payment thresholds are listed here in USD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="769dc-123">一部の市場では、相当する現地通貨が使用されます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-123">In some markets, the equivalent in local currency is used.</span></span> 

- [<span data-ttu-id="769dc-124">Microsoft Store</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-124">Microsoft Store</span></span>](#microsoft-store)
- [<span data-ttu-id="769dc-125">Microsoft Advertising</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="769dc-125">Microsoft Advertising</span></span>](#microsoft-advertising)
